[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2077[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2078[0m[39m:                goto done;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2079[0m[39m:            *out++ = c;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2080[0m[39m:   [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2081[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2082[0m[39m:                goto done;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2083[0m[39m:   [0m[39m    *out++ = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;36m0xC0[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2084[0m[39m:            *out++ = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2085[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2086[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2087[0m[39m:        in++;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2088[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2089[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2090[0m[39m:    ret = out - outstart;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2091[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m2092:d[0m[39mone:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2093[0m[39m:    *outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2094[0m[39m:    *inlen = in - instart;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2095[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2096[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for Heap-Buffer-Overflow in UTF32ToUTF8[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability in `encoding.[0m[1;92mc:2868[0m[39m` is a **missing bounds check** in the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF32ToUTF8` function. This function converts UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m encoded input to UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m output[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut fails to verify that sufficient space exists in the output buffer before [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting, causing a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Missing Components:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. No `outend` pointer calculation to mark the output buffer boundary[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. No bounds checks before any of the four write operations [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m-byte, and [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte writes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Incorrect `inend` calculation using `& ~[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` instead of `& ~[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` for [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malignment[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Evidence from Codebase:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other conversion functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`UTF16LEToUTF8`, `UTF16BEToUTF8`, `latin1ToUTF8`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF8ToUTF32`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m properly implement bounds checking[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These functions follow a consistent pattern: calculate `outend`, check before [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meach write, use `goto done` for clean exit[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Fix Implementation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must be applied to `[0m[35m/src/libxml2/[0m[95mencoding.c[0m[39m` in the `UTF32ToUTF8` function [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2842[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2919[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add output buffer end pointer calculation**[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Immediately after line [0m[1;36m2848[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter `unsigned char *outstart = out;`[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add: `unsigned char *outend = out + *outlen;`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This establishes the boundary that must not be crossed during writes[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix input buffer alignment**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Line [0m[1;36m2847[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change: `const unsigned char *inend = in + [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*inlen & ~[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To: `const unsigned char *inend = in + [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*inlen & ~[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reason: UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m uses [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes per character, so alignment must be to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundaries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmask with ~[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m not ~[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add bounds check before [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASCII path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Before line [0m[1;36m2868[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto done;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This prevents writing when buffer is full[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Add bounds check before [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte write**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Before line [0m[1;36m2872[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;36m0xC0[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto done;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m bytes are available for [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m sequences[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Add bounds check before [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte write**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Before line [0m[1;36m2877[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;36m0xE0[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto done;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes are available for [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m sequences[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m: Add bounds check before [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte write [0m[1;39m([0m[39msurrogate pair path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Before line [0m[1;36m2904[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c & [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto done;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are available for [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39msurrogate pairs[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m: Add clean exit label**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Location: Replace lines [0m[1;36m2913[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2918[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Current code:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39min-instart > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ret = out - outstart;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*inlen = in - instart;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace with:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mret = out - outstart;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdone:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *inlen = in - instart;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This provides a consistent exit point that always updates output/input lengths [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Consistency with Codebase:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix follows the exact pattern used by `UTF16LEToUTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2227[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2293[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF16BEToUTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2421[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2487[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and `latin1ToUTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2057[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2096[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses the same bounds checking idioms: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout >= outend[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for single writes, `if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < N[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for N-byte writes[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the `goto done` pattern for graceful exit when buffer space is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhausted[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify the UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m to UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion algorithm[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not change the surrogate pair handling logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough it appears to have [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseparate issues, those are not causing the current crash[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only adds safety checks without altering functionality[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses the Vulnerability:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents all potential buffer overflows by checking before every write operation[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The check at line [0m[1;36m2868[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the crash occurs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will catch the exact scenario in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe crash report[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returns `XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE` when buffer is full, allowing the caller to handle [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgracefully[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Impact on Other Code:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function signature and return semantics remain unchanged[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Callers like `xmlCharEncInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mencoding.[0m[1;92mc:1562[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1620[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already handle the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE` return code[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer management functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlBufAddLen`, `xmlBufAvail`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already expect this [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Partial Conversion**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When buffer fills, conversion stops mid-stream[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mitigation: This is the expected behavior - caller can allocate more space or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocess the partial result. The `*inlen` and `*outlen` parameters correctly track [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprogress.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Performance Impact**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Additional bounds checks add minimal overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m conditional branches per [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mitigation: This is negligible compared to the bit manipulation operations [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready performed. Security correctness takes precedence over micro-optimization.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Input Alignment Fix**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changing `& ~[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` to `& ~[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` may process fewer bytes if input length is not [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maligned[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mitigation: This is correct behavior - UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m characters MUST be [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte aligned. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe previous code was incorrect and could read past buffer boundaries.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix is directly modeled after:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `UTF16LEToUTF8` at encoding.[0m[1;92mc:2227[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2293[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnearly identical structure[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `UTF16BEToUTF8` at encoding.[0m[1;92mc:2421[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2487[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `latin1ToUTF8` at encoding.[0m[1;92mc:2057[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2096[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimpler but same principle[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `UTF8ToUTF32` at encoding.[0m[1;92mc:2738[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2840[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreverse direction, shows correct bounds [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these functions demonstrate that bounds checking is the standard practice in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibxml2's encoding conversion layer, and UTF32ToUTF8 was simply missing this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical safety mechanism.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing Considerations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be validated against:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The original crashing testcase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshould no longer overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Valid UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m documents with various character ranges [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASCII, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m-byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge cases: buffer exactly full, buffer with [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes remaining[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Large documents that require multiple conversion chunks[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mixed endianness UTF-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m documents[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
